 hyderabad kii apni badminton academy ke ground floor par bani gym kii ek bench par bharat ke mukhya rashtriya coach 40 varshiya pulela gopichand or unki sabase honhaar shishyaaon main se ek 18 varshiya pusarala venkat sindhu saath-saath baithe hai
 Sindhu ranks among the top 15 players in the world in women's badminton
 donon is bare main baatcheet kar rahe hai ki is khel ne kis tarah se ek aakaar liya, kis tarah se uskaa vikaas hua
 Senior Editor Amarnath K
 menon ke saath ek mulaakaat main unhone 1980 ke ol england championships main prakaash padukon kii jeet par charchaa kii
 It also became a matter of discussion how Gopichand failed to make an impact until the emergence of his fast young disciple Saina Nehwal despite Padukone's feat in 2001
 or kyon aakhir sindhu ek ubhartee hui star hai
 Since the time of Pullela Gopichand Prakash Padukone sir, India's badminton game has been run on the same player
 unhone 1980 kii ol england championships samet kai khitaab jite
 After a decade, it seemed that there is no longer any special attraction in this game
 magar 1990 ke dashak main logon kii dilchaspee ek baar phir se jagane lagi
 After that i got a chance and in 2001 suddenly i also won the All England Championship
 magar main zyada samay tak chotii par na rah sakaa
 Far from breaking the other records made by Prakash sir, i could not even match them
 chot or kuch duusari vajahon se mujhe bahut zyada maukey bhi nahin mil paae
 After that there was a bad phase
 magar 2008 main sina nehwal ne ummiden phir se jagaa deen
 But it was not as good for Indian badminton as it was for Saina
 pichley saal hamane sindhu ko asian junior champion banate dekha or is saal unhen malaysian grand pricks jitate or vishwa championships main bhi ek padak jitate dekha
 After this, people were forced to pay serious attention to Indian badminton
 yah ek nai shuruyaat isliye he kyonki ab hamaara yah khel ek hi vyakti ke ird-gird simata nahin rahaa
 This is the reason that in the run-up to the Indian Badminton League earlier this year, the audience was heard commenting on the changing mood of the game
 yahi ki badminton ab yahaan ek paripakv avasthaa main aata dikh rahaa he
 Pusarla Venkat Sindhugopi Sir, it seems that in your era, it would have been very different to have a career in sports
 yah bataaie ki us vakt kii mukhya chunautiyaan aakhir kya thim?gopichand1980 ke dashak kii shuruyaat main 1982 ke asian khelon tak kaaphi had tak cricket ko or thodaa-bahut hockey ko protsaahan or praayojak mil rahe the
 Apart from cricket, the total effort and money spent on the promotion of other sports and building infrastructure used to be a minor part of the effort and money spent in the field of cricket
 lekin cricket ke saath kisi bhi tarah kii tulana bemaani he
 All this has changed in the last two decades
 hamaari suvidhaon or prashikshan kaushal kii tulana is khel main duniya kii kuch sarvshereshth suvidhaon or prashikshan kaushal se kii ja sakati he
 But yes, there is still no appetite for Olympic gold medal as it should be in a big country like India
 is maamle main shaayad hamen china se sabak lenaa hoga
 China's challenge in badminton is very strong in Sindhuaj's date
 agar aap unke kisi khilaadi ke khilaaf khel rahe hai to yah bilkul hi alag tarah kaa khel ho jaataa he
 It must have been even more difficult to face world class competitors in your time
 gopichanddekhie, aap agar badminton main kuch acha karnaa chaahate hai to aapako chiniyon ko pachhadia hi hoga
 a great wall of China is also in the area of badminton
 sina ne chiniyon ke khilaaf khele lagbhag 60 gemon main har teen main se sirf ek game hi jeeta he
 P
 in men
 kashyap unke khilaaf khele gaye har paanch main se sirf ek game hi jeet paae hai
 There are five Indians in the top 25 players in the world in men's and women's badminton, while China has seven players and all of them are in the top 10 players
 ve sachmuch jabardast hai
 At the moment Sindhu's record is superb as she has won half of her matches played against the Chinese
 sindhuunaka kamitment sachmuch dekhne laayak he
 His strategy and his way of elevating his game in difficult moments makes him a better player than others
 kabhi-kabhi ve shuruyaat main hi kuch points de dene kaa prayaas karte hai taaki ham khush hokar apni ekaagratha kho baithen
 Gopichandmagar Sindhu is not much stuck in this trap
 aisa isliye ho sakaa he kyonki ham bhi apane virodhiyon ke khilne ke tareeke kaa adhyayan kar rahe hai, use record kar rahe hai or ek-ek khilaadi se nibatane ke liye jaruri sudhaar kar rahe hai
 Here, yoga and meditation help a lot
 mujhe yaad he ki mere mata-pita subah 4
 Used to wake me up at 30 and traveled about 30 kilometers and used to leave me to the academy
 yah mere liye bahut kathin tha kyonki mujhe skool kii class chhodmai padati thi or phir mujhe maansik prashikshan pasand nahin tha
 i used to think that just playing badminton is enough
 uske baad gopi sar ne kaman sanbhali or mujhe or kai duusare khiladinnon ko bilkul badal diya
 Gopichand: That's because after winning the All England Championship in 2001, i decided that a lot more needs to be done for badminton by arranging facilities and training from a scientific point of view
 2003 main andhra pradesh sarkaar ne academy shuru karne ke liye 45 saal ke patte par mujhe paanch acre chattani jameen di
 But he did not have the money to develop it
 karj lene ke liye mujhe apni paariwarik sampatti girvee rakhni padi
 By 2008, with the help of Yonex and a relative, we developed it into an academy equipped with all kinds of facilities
 sindhumere mata-pita donon rashtriya basketbaal khilaadi rahe hai or ve logon ko bataate aae hai ki kaise unki yuvavastha ke dinon main kisi bhi khel ke liye prashikshan suvidhaon kaa nitant abhaav hua karata tha
 And they tell me that by coming from Secunderabad and settling at a distance of 2 km from the academy, i was able to make the most of the facilities here
 gopichandmujhe lagata he ki purna samarpan pehali jarurat he
 This is the reason why i get everyone to strictly follow the time table and training rules
 aisi mul pravritiyaan hi drudh sankalp kaa nirmaan karti hai
 There are no two opinions that no two players are alike
 alag maansikta, alag deal-doll, shaareerik kad-lathi or khel kii ek vyaktigat style ke saath har khilaadi apane aap main anoothaa hota he
 a comprehensive training program is important in which you develop speed, agility and fitness, etc
 sindhukhel main takat laane ke liye mujhe chocolate chhodkar spirulina kaa haraa powder, si-vid or kuch duusare aahaar lene pade
 Many more sacrifices like this are part of hard training
 filmein dekhne ke moh par thodaa lagaam lagaana bhi isamen shaamil he
 Gopichand: We have also started reaping a good crop from a rich nursery of players
 sindhu kii hi tarah bhartiya khiladinnon kii ek yuva paudh he jo behatar pradarshan kar rahi he or uske achche nattejey dene main mahaj ek-do saalon kii der or he
 Apart from the individual players, i am sure that some pairs of our doubles will soon start making a tremendous impression
 sindhuindian badminton lig (ibl) ek shandaar anubhav rahaa he or isse yah khel focus main aayaa he
 Gopi sir, do you think this kind of experiment is going to be useful in the long run? Gopichand This is a tremendous opportunity
 ibl badminton ko aaj kii tulana main or adhik lokapriy banane main yogadan diya ja saktaa he
 But this is not the only thing
 duniya ke sarvshereshth khiladinnon ke saath or unke khilaaf khelte hue hamaare zyada se zyada khiladinnon ko pratispardhaa kaa anubhav miltaa he
 It is a pleasant experience to see the best players playing badminton
 ham kareeb se unki ranneetiyon kaa adhyayan kar sakate hai
 It serves as a learning ground for the future

 kaa ghaataa hua he

 pichley teen vitt varsh main india post kaa ghaataa badhkar 150 fisadi kii badhat hui he

 ek sutara ne kaha, 'board ko injamaam ke maamle main ab tak safalataa nahin mili he kyonki vah apane vyavsaay or dharmik gatividhiyon ko lekar vyast he or vah puure samay team ke saath rahane kii sthiti main nahin he

 ) Rajendra Rao was an engineer by profession, but his mind was full of stories
 mashiinon ke bich rahete hue unke dimag main kahaniyon ke plat ghoomte
 When he started writing stories in the seventh decade, he became a storyteller on the pages of weekly Hindustan, Dharmyuga, Sarika, Kahani, Sunday etc
 sahityakaron kii sohabat kaa man hua to paas main bindki pahunch jate sohanlal dvivedi ke paas
 His memoirs written on him in the last days are very bad
 man hua to kathakaar shivamurti ke aagrah par unke gaanv ho aae
 Enjoying the fragrance of the soil of Awadh, he wrote a deep glossy on it
 kolkata kii khushboo unhen un varjit galiyon main bhi le gayi, jahaan pahunch kar unhone us varjit jivan kii anek maarmik kahaniyaan likhin or vahiin se unka yash paravaan chadha
 Till now, dozens of his story collections have been published, including the use of untruths, novices, rest of the journey, milk teeth, crucifix above sej piya ki, kolai bhai na ashes, paap sansa pyaar hai, how many heads are the core of your lab
 us rehguzar kii talash he ke reportajon main drishyon or sambandhon ko pakadaney kii unki baariki dekhi ja sakati he, to unke upanyaason main alag si khushboo aati he
 With the novel 'na Ghar Mein Na Ghar Tera', he also knocked in the novel world, but overall his story was heavy on all these
 haal main ek naatak 'saint aaf mani' kaa draft bhi puraa kiya he
 Now he is referred to the color directors
 idhar do-teen saal se ve laptaap par likhane lage hai par aaj bhi ve haath se likhe ko sabase behatar maanate hai
 He says, "there should be a lot of convenience for laptops, but there is still a fascination with pen and medicine
" kabhi jab man nahin maanata to dhund letaa hum
 “there was a time when people used to look for stories of coal bhai na ash
 koyala bhai naa raakh: katha shrinkhalakoyala bhai na raakh kii katha shrinkhalaaon ke bare main rajendra raav bataate hai: ''lekhakon kaa jivan vidambnaa se mukt nahin hota
 From cashiness to puberty, my mind kept melting at the people around me who left no stone unturned to decorate their lives
 pahaad khodne ko bhi taiyaar rahe magar raaton kii siyaahi ke sivaa kuch na mila
 The dream continued to shatter like glass toys and there was no hope
 maine likhnaa shuru kiya to inako katha charitron ke rup main dhalta gaya or unki dukhaant gaathaayen likh kar sochaa ki chalo antatogatva maine unka dukh baant liya
 "this story series appeared in the weekly Hindustan by the name of 'coal Bhai Na Rakh' and managed to grab the attention of the readers
 prakashkon kaa bhi
 This was to take the direction of creativity by feeling the sufferings of others at the level of cognition
 lekin, jab baad main, bahut baad main mere par dukh kaa pahaad tutaa to mujhe thik se pataa chalaa ki vah sab, koyala bhai na raakh ke paatr kaise asay pidaa ko jhelte hue jindagi bitaate honge
 There is also an interesting anecdote about the publication of this book
 raav bataate hai, ''un dinon main ek nayaa lekhak tha
 After reading one of my stories, Manohar Shyam Joshi, the editor of the weekly Hindustan, said that give us ten such stories which we will print serially
 'koyala bhai na raakh kii kahaniyaan raajapaal prakaashan ke swami vishwanath ji ko itani pasand ain ki unhone use pustak ke rup main prakashit karne kaa prastaav bheja
 Rajpal was a big publisher in those days
 ek nae lekhak ke liye yah apane aap main ek bada protsaahan tha
 The book was printed and very good royalty was also received
 yah san 1975 kii baat he
 How did the then editors and publishers encourage and inspire young writers
 " kaaphi dinon tak aprakashit rahane ke baad ab yah kitaab pun: raajapaal and sans se prakashit hokar aa gai he
 For some people, story writing is an hour or two-hour game
 aksar aae din chhapane vaale kathakaron ko dekh kar yah anumaan lagaana kathin na hoga
 But in May 2019, it took him a long time to write the story 'sit Jao' which came in the new Gyanodaya
 ve kehete hai, ''pichley chaar dashakon main, kisi kahani ko likhane main itani kathinaayee kabhi nahin hui jitani savitri-satyawan kii is darun gaatha ko kaagaj par utaarne main anubhav hui
 For this, there should be a temple of stone
 '' abhi haal hi main unki charchit kahani 'chokher bali' kaa manchan dilli ke kamaani auditorium main hua jiskaa nirdesan tikam joshi ne kiya
 Rajendra Rao's hobbies Rajendra Rao's hobbies are unique
 apane ghar ke anjir va sharife ko ve bahut yaad karte hue kehete hai, ve kehete hai sharafat kaa nur, hamaare bageeche main
 For example, Sharafat should also be a part of this writer's character
 ve aksar padhane-likhane main mashgool rahete hai
 First wife, then an all-time colloquial companion
 jab se ve nahin hai, ve shabdon se hi gapshap main lage rahete hai
 Sometimes they express this loneliness too
 naatakon main unki dilchaspee bahut he
 They like Ghalib
 samay samay par ai filmon main jo pasand aati hai un par sankshipt tippaniyan likhte hai
 He is also very interested in film songs and chero-poetry
 kabhi koi kitaab pasand ai to vah unke pathan-pathan main rahi
 If you like it very much then write a comment on it and hang it on Facebook
 kabhi vijay kishor maanav ne kadambini ke liye unase kanpur ke sansmaran likhwaaye to unhone bade pyaar se likhaa
 Stitching the memories of Muradnagar neatly
 kanpur main ab se pehle armapur main rahaa karte the
 When he had to leave, he remembered him while passing by later
 vah ghar bhale hi chuta par yaaden vismrit nahin huin
 After reaching there, he remembered everything like, "do we ever go back and go, to the settlement that i had left after years ago - with a heavy heart
" jahaan beete rumaan or rachanaatmakataa main duube hue kuch avismaraneey baras
 This is friends - E-51, Near Sub Station, Armapur, Kanpur-10
 bahut gulzaar or bharaapura ashiana tha yah un dinon
 Away from the metropolis of the metropolis and the untouched Armapur, it was green, picturesque and quiet, not only well-organized
 dwitiya vishwa yuddh ke samay angrejon dwaara aayudh nirmaan ke liye banaai gai yah estate aaj bhi ramnik he
 Yesterday while returning from Panki temple, the train accidentally turned into Armapur
 i-51 gaye, suunaa padaa tha
 "went to an nursery school built in an old bungalow where Shukti first went to the Vidyalaya
 vah skool jaataa to hamaara param vishwast sheru bhi saath jaataa tha or uske lautne tak skool ke baahar hi baitha rahata tha
 An interesting article with photos of both of them was published in Hindustan Weekly
 armapur ke saaf-suthere or atyant anushaasit bazaar main bhi gaye jahaan sab kuch miltaa he
 Fresh vegetables, groceries, clothes, haberdashery, all kinds of chabane which are roasted in a kadhai on a furnace, a goat's meat and chicken passed by a sanitary inspector stamped
 us bazaar kaa drushya adbhut laga
 High-end goods were in front of him with water
 vahaan se liye garmagarm bhune chivade or moongfalee chabate vaapis laute kyonki ab pataa badal jo gaya tha
 "rajendra Rao records every moment of happiness and sorrow with both a bhakta and an observer
" unke bheetar saare maanviya ras maujuud hai
 Every moment has the possibility of a story, like the city is still a possibility for Ashok Vajpayee
 par jaisaa ki kaha he, ve bhale hi tamaam vidhaon ke pathan pathan va lekhan main dilchaspee rakhte hon par hai ve khantee kathakaar hi
 Therefore, he still has his own identity in the story world
 unke pathakon or sampadakon ko aaj bhi unase kahaniyon kii maang bani rahati he
 Easy to see the stories of Rajendra Rao, but a deep-rooted writer in literature, Rajendra Rao has entered a corner of the metropolis of laborers like Kanpur and has made his place on the map of literature
 unki kahaniyon, reportajon kii ek vakt dhooma rahi he
 He has a lot of experience of circling the streets of Kolkata up to pen and despite being associated with the arid world of engineering, he has created and proven many characters, characters and situations in the light of the slow flame of the dream of humanity
 The way life is present everywhere, stories are scattered everywhere, just need to save and capture them
 unki kisi ek bhi kahani se aapkaa guzarana ho to aap rajendra raav ke lekhkeey mijaaz ko shiddat se samaj sakate hai
 Story and poetry also have their own fashion and their own era
 kabhi-kabhi lagata he tamaam kavi prem kavitaayen likh rahe hai to zyaadaatar kathakaar prem kahaniyaan
 The spring of love poems and stories is a mustard
 par kuch kathakaar aise hote hai, jo jitani acchhee prem kahaniyaan likhte hai, jivan main duusare buniyadi pahaluon par bhi utani hi majboot pakad rakhte hai, rajendra raav aise hi kathakaron main hai
 Shocked by every story of his
 duniya masini par bheetar kaa maahaul nihaayat maanviya
 Just a few years ago, after a long silence, Rajendra Rao returned to the world of stories, then reminded him of those days when he used to be among the few famous storytellers of select magazines of the eighties
 71 main kahani patrika main shift kahani ke prakaashan ke baad unhone peeche mud kar nahin dekha or ek se bad kar ek kahaniyon kii jhadi laga di
 Novice, Shift, Coal Bhai Na Ash, Use of untruth, milk teeth and series of love stories Suli Up Sej Piya Ki etc
 is bich unke do upanyaas bhi aae par kahaniyon main unki gati bani rahi
 In the last four to five years he has written more than fifteen stories in his second innings
 jaisaa ki pehle bhi likh chukaa hum, rajendra raav kii ek duniya mecanical ejineering se judi duniya bhi rahi he jahaan unhone mashiinon ke bich kaam kiya, roji roti kamai or duniya jahaan ke anubhav hasil kiye
 His mind may not have seemed between those machines, but he raised many stories from the middle of that mechanical life and created such a rare atmosphere in the story that no ordinary storyteller could reach
 rajendra raav ne prem kii bhi tamaam kahaniyon likhin
 In the next birth, after death, Sudha and Suresh do not turn around, look at the shadows of love, love will take heartache, there are similar stories beyond sin and virtue
 inamen prem kii vikalataa bhi he, kaishorya kaa chhalakta pyaar bhi, prem main likhe gaye lambey lambey patr bhi, aahen bhi or aansu bhi
 The real thing is that their characters do not succumb to the frame of idealism but are seen to transcend the boundaries of taboos
 kintu jahaan apni kahaniyon main unhone premiyon ke dilon kii sookshm scanning kii he, vahiin masini dincharya ke bich se jivan ke anek moolyawaan lamhe bhi uthaae hai
 The study of science and engineering may be dull, but in this world there is a lot of human sympathy even within the grown man
 balki aaj ke daur main tamaam kavi kathakaar, vigyaan takneekee or prabadhan kii duniya se hi aa rahe hai jo abhivyakti kii nai jameen tod rahe hai
 Rajendra Rao worked as an engineer in the factory, being in charge round the clock, it was natural to flaunt his sensitive mind while indulging in the math of machine noise and profit and loss of production
 rajendra raav ke is kathasanchayan kii zyaadaatar kahaniyaan bhi unke inhen anubhavon kii upaj he
 But they say, being in a mechanical world does not mean that there are no colors of interpersonal relationships or that there is no love, no sensation, no life in that world
 balki is tathy ko ham shift, nausikhia, baaki itihaas, ghuspaith or lowki kaa tel aadi kahaniyon main puure vaibhav ke saath dekh pate hai
 The story does not belong to everyone
 ghatana ke varnan ke saath saath paatro ke manobhaavon ko bhi hoobahoo andaaj main rakhte janaa ki jisamen kahanikar kii apni drushti bhi muhaavarey kii bhashaa main dikhti chale, aisa kam hota he
 Where it happens, the story continues to fascinate us along with its text
 udhaaharan ke liye uttaradhikaar main pita paropkaaree swabhaav ke hai
 They send some food items to a disabled person regularly through the son, who keeps getting congested with the road construction in the city and does not take much
 bete ne jab pitaaji kaa riference diya tabhi chijen leen
 But in the end, after the death of the father comes to give him something and then the communication between them opens his eyes
 jaise paroapkaar kii bhaavana putr ko uttaradhikaar main mili ho
 In this, the sentence stated on promotion is noteworthy: "it is the most awaited moment of self-realization in the life of any job profession
 "lowki kaa tel main ek majdoor apane takiya kalam jo he so vaali adaa main bolta hua kitna sahaj lagata he: babu aap shahari aadmi nahin jaanate, ki lowki kaa tel kitna phydemand hota he
 
 
 
 haa haa tel inkaa asli he, paisa bhale hi zyada, jo he so anthte hon
 The protagonist of the story, referring to the relationship between Daaru and chicken choli Daman in Vediki violence, tried to be carnivorous a few times, but when the entrails started coming out, i caught the meat and friends from the hometown
 ek chaat kii dukaan kaa patta pakadte hue anubhav kaisaa hota he suniyeh khaane se pehle hi bheja tar ho jaataa he
 a strange longing arises, which can only be compared to pure lust
 puri kii puri vaidiki hinsa kahani aisi chust muhabaredaari se bhari he
 Thanga, Lundure, Labhed, Nautankibaj, Khalas, Suptan Paurush have to read the vocabulary of the storyteller
 ek jagah isi kahani main aata he, ‘isamen andeh nahi ki upree taur par uskaa aagrah vishuddh rup se ahimsak tha, lekin usamen gandhiji ke satyagrah jaisi pavitrataa nahin thi
 'in the rest of the history, which discusses the director's visit and gm's corruption, see the story of the protagonist who is preparing for the visit - "overnight, the frustration and fearlessness of my love failed and the end came
 The screen flashed like a steel plate
 " shift main kahani kaa nayak kahata he, "main bhi sharir ko plant kii tarah khol dena chahta tha
 "rajendra Rao's stories are not simple stories, stories related to life and society
 ye milon kii, kaarkaanon kii kahaniyaan hai to rishton kii, prem kii, jaddojehad kii, paroapkaar kii, sanskaron ke uhapoh kii, bhartiya yatraaon kii, mecanical life kii, raatapali kii ranginiyon or swamibhakton main kutton si harakat par utar aate manushyon kii kahaniyaan hai
 Every story is written for some purpose
 uskaa har vaakya anubhav kii lambii tapasya se niklaa he
 As much as the story's narration and praise are less appreciated
 rajendra raav vyangyakaar to nahin kintu unke naireshan main kahin kahin shrilaal shukla jaise chust or furtile vaakya chamakate hai
 As Shree Lal Ji has said in Visrampur saint: Government dead spend a lot
 rajendra raav kii kahaniyon main bhi aise vaakya dur se hi chamakate dikhte hai
 In the Vaidiki violence, the storyteller says, "let the sense of drunkenness be with the wine, the chicken is made to be blown, the grand celebration is done, the crucifixion is the first thing in this khatkarma
" " kehane kii baat nahin ki rajendra raav ne apni kissagoi main is saundaryabodh ko kaayam rakhane kaa bharsak praytn kiya he taaki na to ub kaa srijan ho, na saundaryabodh kaa kshay
 The stories of Rao, who kept an eye on any event or incident, confuse the readers
 kahaniyon main prathampurushapraay: unki kahaniyaan pratham purush main likhi gayi hai, jinamein khud kathakaar kii shakhsiyat bolti he
 He is motivated by a duty of obedience as an obedient son (succession), while on a waiting ticket in a train while traveling illegally and using untruths as a passenger (using untruth), somewhere on duty in shift
 So a newbie in the factory somewhere
 kahin jivan kii choti se choti safalataa ko celibratt karne kii manshaa rakhane vaale shakhsah ke rup main (vaidiki hinsa) to kahin nimna madhya vargeey jivan main khatate hue yuvak ke rup main (lowki kaa tel), kahin apni corporate kii naukari se ajiz aakar premika ke pita ke saath koching kaa dhandha aajamaane kii koshish main lage ravi jaise (amar nahi yah pyaar), to kahin naukari ke liye sangharsh karte chhinnomasta ke satish ke rup main
 But the female characters are also full of human qualities, whether it is the handicap of succession, the mother of gourd oil, the mother of chinnamasta, or not immortal, it is the merit of love anadarsh sthitiyon main bhi unke paatr yaad rah jane vaale, dhiraj na khone vaale paatr hai
 In a society surrounded by evils, there is a dream within them that Rajendra Rao kept alive as a slow flame in every story
 yahi rajendra raav kii kahaniyon kii visheshta he ki ve masini duniya se anubhav ugahte avashya hai kintu uske bheetar ke maanviya pahalu ko najrandaaj nahin karte, sadaiv use kahaniyon ke centre main rakhte hai
